w-100"><p class="text | article-text">LAREDO, Tex. (KGNS) -A small but growing number of central American migrants are making their way north toward the U.S.</p><p class="text | article-text">Economic hardships due to the COVID-19 pandemic are leading these people to leave home and try to reach the United States.</p><p class="text | article-text">In southeastern Mexico, a few dozen members of a caravan waited by train tracks on Tuesday looking to board a freight train north.</p><p class="text | article-text">They had been able to evade Guatemalan soldiers and Mexican border officials along the way.</p><div></div><p class="text | article-text">The Central Americans have spent the last few weeks crisscrossing toward the border after the coronavirus ravaged the already poor region.</p><p class="text | article-text">One hastily organized caravan departed from Honduras two weeks ago.</p><p class="text | article-text">The group initially overwhelmed Guatemalan border security.</p><p class="text | article-text">The Guatemalan government responded by having the army round up and deport more than 3,000 of the migrants back to Honduras.</p><p class="text | article-text"><i>Copyright 2020 KGNS. All rights reserved.</i></p></div></section><section class="recommendations | w-100"><div id="fusion-static-enter:8d92ea94-de48-4d03-85d2-26a9340e8648" style="display:none"></div><div class="connatix | row mb-3"><div class="my-3 col"><div id="connatix-highlights-embed" class="w-100 h-100"><script id="a8e266bfac5841009afeb5359bf68301">

w-100"><p class="text | article-text">LAREDO, Tex. (KGNS) -A small but growing number of central American migrants are making their way north toward the U.S.</p><p class="text | article-text">Economic hardships due to the COVID-19 pandemic are leading these people to leave home and try to reach the United States.</p><p class="text | article-text">In southeastern Mexico, a few dozen members of a caravan waited by train tracks on Tuesday looking to board a freight train north.</p><p class="text | article-text">They had been able to evade Guatemalan soldiers and Mexican border officials along the way.</p><div></div><p class="text | article-text">The Central Americans have spent the last few weeks crisscrossing toward the border after the coronavirus ravaged the already poor region.</p><p class="text | article-text">One hastily organized caravan departed from Honduras two weeks ago.</p><p class="text | article-text">The group initially overwhelmed Guatemalan border security.</p><p class="text | article-text">The Guatemalan government responded by having the army round up and deport more than 3,000 of the migrants back to Honduras.</p><p class="text | article-text"><i>Copyright 2020 KGNS. All rights reserved.</i></p></div></section><section class="recommendations | w-100"><div id="fusion-static-enter:8d92ea94-de48-4d03-85d2-26a9340e8648" style="display:none"></div><div class="connatix | row mb-3"><div class="my-3 col"><div id="connatix-highlights-embed" class="w-100 h-100"><script id="a8e266bfac5841009afeb5359bf68301">
